[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe heap-buffer-overflow occurs in `freerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy` at line [0m[1;36m1570[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `[0m[35m/src/FreeRDP/libfreerdp/crypto/[0m[95mcertificate.c[0m[39m`. The vulnerability has three [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcritical issues:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Primary Issue: Integer Type Overflow**[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m1537[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1539[0m[39m use `uint16_t` for `blocksize`, `offset`, and `length` variables[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maximum value: [0m[1;36m65[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m535[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39m64KB - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Certificate chains commonly exceed this limit in production environments[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- When variables overflow, they wrap around to small values[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Buffer reallocation uses wrapped values, allocating insufficient memory[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Subsequent writes to actual offset positions exceed allocated buffer bounds[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Secondary Issue: Incorrect Loop Condition**[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m1546[0m[39m: `while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstatus != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` checks the previous iteration's BIO_read status[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This can cause the loop to continue when buffer state is invalid[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Correct pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1493[0m[39m in `bio_read_pem`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: `while [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset < length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidates current buffer state[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Tertiary Issue: Missing Safety Check**[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m1513[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1514[0m[39m in the correct `bio_read_pem` implementation include: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- offset > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;`[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This check exits the loop when buffer space remains after a read[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prevents unnecessary reallocations and ensures proper buffer sizing before null [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mterminator write[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The buggy function omits this critical validation[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Code Path Analysis[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is triggered specifically for certificates containing policy OID [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"2.23.140.1.2.1"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRFC [0m[1;36m7299[0m[39m domain validation certificates[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLLVMFuzzerTestOneInput[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓ freerdp_certificate_data_new_from_pem[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓ freerdp_certificate_new_from_pem[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓ freerdp_certificate_data_new_nocopy[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓ freerdp_certificate_data_load_cache[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓ freerdp_certificate_get_pem_ex [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1633[0m[39m: policy check[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓ freerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mVULNERABLE[0m[1;39m][0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase contains a correct reference implementation `bio_read_pem` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1477[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1527[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that uses proper types and loop logic. The buggy function was introduced[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto handle RFC [0m[1;36m7299[0m[39m policy requirements but contains critical implementation flaws.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Fix Implementation Strategy[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Recommended Approach: Remove Redundant Implementation**[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSince there is no functional difference in how PEM data should be read based on [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcertificate policy, the optimal fix is to eliminate the policy-based code path [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentirely.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** `[0m[35m/src/FreeRDP/libfreerdp/crypto/[0m[95mcertificate.c[0m[39m`[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Remove the policy-based conditional [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1631[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1637[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Replace the entire if-else block with a single call to the correct implementation[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Change from:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```c[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Updated rfc to handle specific policy issues[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[4;94mhttps://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc7299[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m [0m[1;35mfreerdp_certificate_policies[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcert, [0m[32m"2.23.140.1.2.1"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mfreerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbio, &pem, pLength[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mbio_read_pem[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbio, &pem, pLength[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- To:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```c[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mbio_read_pem[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbio, &pem, pLength[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Remove the buggy function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1529[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1580[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Delete the entire `freerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy` function[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This function is now unused after Step [0m[1;36m1[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Removing it prevents future accidental usage[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Remove the policy check function if no longer needed**[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Review all usages of `freerdp_certificate_policies` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1351[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1380[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If this was the only call site, consider removing or marking as unused[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This is optional and depends on whether other code paths need policy checking[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This Fix Is Optimal:**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates All Three Root Causes:** [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No integer overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39muses correct implementation with `size_t`[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Correct loop condition preserved[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Safety check remains intact[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic:**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `bio_read_pem` function is already battle-tested[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No functionality changes for non-policy certificates[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Policy-based certificates now use the same safe code path[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Simplifies Codebase:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removes ~[0m[1;36m50[0m[39m lines of duplicate, buggy code[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Eliminates maintenance burden of parallel implementations[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reduces attack surface[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Functional Regression:**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The RFC [0m[1;36m7299[0m[39m comment suggests policy-specific handling was needed[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - However, both functions perform identical operations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreading BIO to char [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Policy information is preserved in the X509 certificate structure[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No evidence that reading PEM data requires policy-specific logic[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Supports All Certificate Sizes:**[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `bio_read_pem` uses `size_t` types supporting multi-MB certificates[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Handles modern certificate chains with many intermediate CAs[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No arbitrary 64KB limit[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Policy-based behavior change:** Certificates with OID [0m[32m"2.23.140.1.2.1"[0m[39m will [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnow use the same code path as others[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation:** This is the intended behavior since no policy-specific reading[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic is required[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Performance impact:** Removes one function call and policy check per [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcertificate[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation:** Positive side effect - slightly faster execution[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Breaking changes:** [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m - the external API remains unchanged[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Both code paths returned the same data structure[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Only the internal implementation changes[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Testing Strategy:**[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Existing unit tests should pass unchanged[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fuzzer should no longer reproduce the crash[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Test with large certificate chains [0m[1;39m([0m[39m>64KB[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Test both policy-matching and non-matching certificates[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Verify PEM data correctness after conversion[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Alternative Approach [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIf Policy Distinction Required[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIf policy-specific handling is absolutely necessary [0m[1;39m([0m[39munlikely based on analysis[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfix `freerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy` by making it identical to `bio_read_pem`:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes needed:**[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m1537[0m[39m: `const size_t blocksize = [0m[1;36m2048[0m[39m;`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m1538[0m[39m: `size_t offset = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;`[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m1539[0m[39m: `size_t length = blocksize;`[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m1546[0m[39m: `while [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset < length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m1532[0m[39m: Move `int status = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;` inside the loop and make it `const int status`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- After line [0m[1;36m1512[0m[39m: Add `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength - offset > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;`[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHowever, this approach is not recommended because it maintains code duplication [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout clear benefit.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m. References from Codebase[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Correct Implementation Pattern:**[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `bio_read_pem` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcertificate.[0m[1;92mc:1477[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1527[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - Reference implementation[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `x509_utils_from_pem` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mx509_utils.[0m[1;92mc:632[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m633[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - Size validation pattern[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Related Structures:**[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `rdp_certificate` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcertificate.[0m[1;92mc:89[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m96[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - Certificate with chain support[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `rdp_certificate_data` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcertificate_data.[0m[1;92mc:37[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m48[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - Cached PEM storage[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Call Sites:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `freerdp_certificate_get_pem_ex` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcertificate.[0m[1;92mc:1587[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1642[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - Where policy check [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccurs[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `freerdp_certificate_data_load_cache` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcertificate_data.[0m[1;92mc:84[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m89[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - Calls [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mget_pem_ex twice [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith and without chain[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
